I couldnâ€™t get in, so I asked the waiter for an extra room card and was told to compensate 30 yuan. This really surprised me. As a listed five-star hotel standard, it costs 30 yuan to get an extra room card. The waiter said that if they didnâ€™t charge 30 yuan, they would have to pay 30 yuan themselves.
I have stayed in other five-star hotels around the world for decades, and the hotel has never argued with guests about paying 30 yuan for missing room cards. If you want one or two more, you can give it at will, and itâ€™s okay if you accidentally take it away. Home Inn has never asked guests to pay 30 yuan for room cards.

Shanwei Wyndham Hotel is really a hotel management standard thinking of the 1980s, and if you donâ€™t see it, you will lose money.

I never write bad reviews for hotels I've stayed in, but after thinking for a long time, I decided to write down the true experience. First, I'm a local, and I hope my hometown can become more civilized and progressive, and have a good five-star hotel. Second, I don't want the backward service thinking of this Wyndham Hotel to have a negative impact on foreign guests, and don't slap the face of Haifeng people.

I hope the owner of this hotel can see my message, and can develop a big business in Haifeng, and don't care about small money anymore.

OK, it doesn't matter, there are still plenty of parking spaces in the underground garage, and I don't mind walking a few more steps)

Third, the hygiene of the room was worrying, there were many hairs on the headrest of the bed, and thick dust

Fifth, when I went to the gym, the front desk staff also ignored me and seemed unwilling to turn on the lights for us to use

Objectively speaking, Wyndham Xiamen is really great. The staff are polite and proactive. However, the development of Shanwei City has determined that the service awareness of people cannot keep up with the requirements of the brand. The experience is too bad! The service attitude is not even as good as the homestays in Nan'ao Island, Shantou. If you don't raise awareness and broaden your horizons, it will only drag down the brand.
